results both in analytical form, based on control intervals defined by the user, both in graphic form 2D, developed for computers with low performance, so as to expand its range of compatible hardware, and in both three-dimensional field for 3D impact more pleasant and accommodating of the simulated network.\r\n\r\nReady for research\r\nTritone was built primarily from research and
